    <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2336623" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2336623" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="valkyriee"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2053372"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2053372.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="valkyriee" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2336623ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2336623" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2053372">valkyriee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-03"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730647130" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't know about this one. It's very well made, it stands out. <br />
<br />
However it is very very popular among a lot of men in my environment. Either they're heavy sprayers or that scent alone is too strong.<br />
<br />
I think I only ever liked it once on someone - it was very cold outside, so mixed with the super cold air, it was smelling almost like fresh roses and light woods. Pleasant. Not too strong but definitely projecting.<br />
All the other times I have smelt this, it's too much. Based on skin chemistry on some friends even too sweet. Too sweet, too cloying, too strong. Very suffocating, if oversprayed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2336623"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2336623#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2334905" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Perhaps after Black Orchid’s groundbreaking breakthrough in the perfumery world, this perfume is the peak of the interest in Middle Eastern scent culture, which was previously underestimated by Westerners. <br />
<br />
A perfume that makes you feel luxurious with its extraordinary powerful performance and layered structure that you can feel with every sniff. I don’t think its scent is extraordinary, but it is a work that stands out with its great quality in the world of luxury perfumes. Ombre Nomade has a refined, sophisticated and yet complex aura.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2334905"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2334905#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2334270" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The composition is linear throughout the very long life of this masterpiece and the oud used is unanimous within the community of perfume lovers in Europe and beyond since I have never heard a negative review about this perfume other than its price. From YSL M7 by Tom Ford in 2002 to Ombre nomade 16 years later, European perfume lovers have evolved and gradually become accustomed to the smell of oud and this perfume, through the success it has had, is the perfect illustration of that evolution.<br />
4 to 5 sprays max preferably during cold season and you are good to go for the entire day with this beast. A similar fragrance is The Moon by Frederic Malle which I prefer but only a few connoisseurs will notice the difference in the air while the price point of the moon is really high as compared to Ombre nomade which is a great perfume in a refillable bottle (long term economies of scales😊😉). 8.25/10 in my book.📝📓😊</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Masculine decent fragrance but still can be wear by all. Its an middle east fragrance so obiviouly its lasting power and overall performance would be two times than french and european perfumes.<br />
<br />
Opening is very strong for 15 minuts and dominated by combo of safron and raspberry. Afterwards its slighly toned down but still on the beast projection for first 1.5-2. hours. Personally I smell throughout the performance is safron with slight touch of rose (in decent way) and oud not being animalic. I got many compliments for this.<br />
<br />
Its longevity is 10+ hours with just 3-4 sprays along with moderate sillage. So I would recommended not to overpray it in indoor area. For going to open places you can wear 6-7 sprays which is enough. And on clothes, you can smell till next 4-5 days even.<br />
<br />
Rating:<br />
Scent - 10/10<br />
Longevity - 9.5/10<br />
Projection - 9.5/10<br />
Price - 5/10<br />
Overall - 8.50/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2308641"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2308641#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2308612" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2306036" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Eau de Cornichon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1753083"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1753083.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Eau de Cornichon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Santal-Blush-12766.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12766.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Santal Blush"title="Santal Blush"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2306036ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2306036" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1753083">Eau de Cornichon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 14:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is not a revolutionary scent profile. Leather, oud, rose and saffron are a very common combination of notes in middle eastern perfumery, but it's a tricky thing to nail.<br />
<br />
Ombré Nomade is a fantastic take on this idea. It's tame, smooth, well balanced, attractive and 100% in line with the brand. <br />
<br />
I've seen some commenters claiming that has a harsh, fecal opening, and frankly, these people are out of their minds. <br />
There's a bit of an oily funk in the first couple of minutes, but it's NOTHING compared to even the mildest of barnyard ouds or animalic musks.<br />
<br />
This is a very safe, easy to wear leather - oud, the leather isn't too far off from a Tom Ford leather, neither is the oud accord, the saffron is loud and metallic, there's quite a bit of smoke, the rose and raspberry are a bit jammy but relatively subtle. You can easily make out the notes but it's quite rounded, nothing sticks out like a sore thumb. <br />
<br />
This isn't the end all be all leather - oud, but it's a fantastic scent and my favorite release from Louis Vuitton that I've tried so far.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The rose/raspberry mixed with oud is so luxurious and heavenly. This scent just makes you feel like a Big Bawse. Definitely something to wear for formal occasions or if you just want to stand out from the crowd. Put this on if your self-esteem is low, thank me later.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2292609"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2292609#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288757" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1526621">Fresca</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-19">09/19/24 20:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is impressive.  We've been wearing way too many perfumes in our house lately.  You name it, we've been overspraying it.  We're a little nose blind.  But I put one teeny tiny little spray of Ombre Nomade on my wrist, and it cut through everything else.  LV is not messing about with this.  <br />
<br />
Ombre Nomade is essentially a dark rose/oud combo.  Everyone has probably smelled something like it before.  But even though Ombre Nomade isn't original, it is much better than most other fragrances in this category.  It's bigger and softer and smoother; I think even if you're not an oud fan you just might be persuaded by this.  <br />
<br />
It's too masculine for me personally (it's the leather.  The leather gets kinda loud in the dry down).  I prefer Dior's Oud Ispahan.  Not a safe blind buy, especially not at LV prices.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2288757"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2288757#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288512" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2288088" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Apotheosis"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1782562"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Apotheosis" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2288088ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2288088" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1782562">Apotheosis</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-19">09/19/24 08:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ombre Nomad makes its entrance like a dramatic flourish at the opera, sweeping in with a heady mix of oud, rose, and incense that nearly rattles the senses. It's the olfactory equivalent of a velvet smoking jacket—bold, assertive, and dripping with confidence. Yet, for all its swagger, it treads familiar ground. The category is crowded, and let’s be honest—there are more affordable options that whisper the same sweet nothings to your nose.<br />
<br />
This fragrance doesn’t tiptoe; it strides in, fully aware of its presence, commanding attention. It's not one for the office, nor any setting where subtlety is required—here, you’ll be smelt long before you’re seen. That said, the raspberry note does add a playful wink, offering a twist on the usual suspects. It may not be a groundbreaking scent, but it’s certainly one with character.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2288088"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2288088#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2284806" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The raspberry is very prominent in the beginning. After about 30-40 minutes it’s very beautifully blended. I don’t get a barnyard oud at all in this but if you aren’t used to oud it might be harsh. Really good though. Grown, 25+ imo. You will be noticed with this. It’s dark. Which is right up my alley. If you like bright uplifting fragrances this isn’t for you. Anyone can wear anything but I believe you need a certain type of confidence for this. You need to be comfortable in your own skin because again, this is a head turner. It’s worth every penny. This is for date night and formal events. Please do not wear this in high heat. Fall and Winter is where this shines. <br />
<br />
P.S. do not go to the lv store and spray this on a card. You have to try it on skin to understand what you’re getting out of this scent. And in the air people around you will pickup more Amber. Close to skin you pickup more of the smoky accord. Hope this helps!<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2276059"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2276059#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272016" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2272016" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Zongo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559457"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1559457.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Zongo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2272016ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2272016" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559457">Zongo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 23:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Prick up your ears, you odor-obsessed orangutans! If you haven't experienced Louis Vuitton's Ombre Nomade, you're missing out on an olfactory odyssey that'll make your previous scent adventures feel like a kiddie pool splash party.<br />
<br />
This isn't just a fragrance, it's a one-way ticket to the outer reaches of aromatic bliss. The moment this liquid gold hits your skin, you're strapped to a runaway camel, galloping full-tilt through a kaleidoscopic desert of the senses.<br />
<br />
The oud in this beast isn't your run-of-the-mill, watered-down nonsense. No sir, this is the real deal - the kind of oud that'd make a Bedouin sheikh weep tears of joy. It's like someone distilled the very essence of a thousand-year-old forest and bottled it up for our twisted pleasure.<br />
<br />
And just when you think you've got a handle on this scent rodeo, the incense kicks in. Suddenly, you're floating on a cloud of holy smoke, ascending to a higher plane of existence where mere mortals fear to tread.<br />
<br />
But wait, there's more! A hint of raspberry sneaks in like a cat burglar, adding a touch of sweetness to this wild ride. It's like finding a perfectly ripe berry in the middle of the Sahara - unexpected, but goddamn delightful.<br />
<br />
The longevity on this juice? Eternal, my friends. You could wear this stuff through a nuclear winter and still come out smelling like the king of the wasteland. And the sillage? It's got more projection than a drive-in movie theater. You'll leave a scent trail so magnificent, people will be following you like the Pied Piper of Hamelin.<br />
<br />
Is it synthetic? Maybe a touch. But who gives a flying frog's fat ass when it smells this good? It's like complaining about the brushstrokes on the Mona Lisa.<br />
<br />
In a world of cookie-cutter scents and play-it-safe perfumery, Ombre Nomade stands tall as a beacon of olfactory rebellion. It's not for the faint of heart or the weak of nose. But for those brave enough to take the plunge, it's a one-way ticket to scent nirvana.<br />
<br />
So strap in, spray liberally, and prepare for a fragrant journey that'll make your head spin and your nostrils sing. Because in this cruel circus of life, sometimes you need to smell like you've been riding a magic carpet through a forest fire in paradise.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2242114" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Trench1419!"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169860"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2169860.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Trench1419!" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Myriad-85363.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.85363.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Myriad"title="Myriad"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2242114ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2242114" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169860">Trench1419!</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-07">08/07/24 16:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't think I've written a review for Ombre Nomade yet; it's one of my favorite fragrances that I've tried so far. It was just the second bottle of Louis Vuitton fragrance that I bought, after Pacific Chill.<br />
<br />
I had gotten a free sample of Ombre Nomade, when I bought Pacific Chill. I had heard such praise for this fragrance, and seen it in the "Business Insider" video about oud, along with Tom Ford Oud Wood.<br />
<br />
I wouldn't say that Ombre Nomade was a "love at first smell" for me, like Pacific Chill or LOVERS or Nuit de Feu or Attrape-Reves were, but I could tell that it was a rich, deep, complex scent, and I definitely liked it right away. <br />
<br />
I was still so new to fragrances and trying to detect the different fragrance notes and everything, but I've grown a lot since then and worn Ombre Nomade many times, by itself and layered with other scents. I can't tell you exactly how it smells, but I love it. I love how I can use a few sprays in the morning before work, and still smell that rich leather and oud all day long. <br />
<br />
I wore it the other day, and the lady at the dispensary said I smelled amazing, so that was nice. The one time a random stranger stopped me and asked what fragrance I had used, because I smelled so amazing, was when I was with my now ex fiance at the grocery store. I had layered Ombre Nomade, Pacific Chill, and Mancera Instant Crush.<br />
<br />
One of my favorite layering combinations is Attrape-Reves and Ombre Nomade, because of how the fresh, light, fruity floral aroma in Attrape-Reves compliment the rich leather and oud in Ombre Nomade.  I had initially bought Attrape-Reves to give to my ex fiance, but she ghosted me again so I've just been using it myself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2242114"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2242114#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2241576" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It makes me VERY curious about their other fragrances. Do they have others in this same vein?<br />
My lady has a great nose and this fragrance drives her absolutely NUTS. She huffs it off me like a glue addict. Always a good sign. It also plays off my chemistry well. <br />
While it may be a bit intense for a hot summer day, it's great for that hot night. The rose, Raspberry, amber and saffron make it great for a summer evening. It's sexy, spicy-animalic, playful, sophisticated. Great for date night. <br />
The longevity is mental, the sillage is great and it is a compliment magnate, especially from the ladies. It has an androgynous character that really provides a great juxtaposition to a more classically masculine dressed man. <br />
I have a decant but will definitely be getting a bottle at some point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2238819"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2238819#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2236323" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2230048" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Trench1419!"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169860"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2169860.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Trench1419!" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Myriad-85363.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.85363.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Myriad"title="Myriad"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2230048ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2230048" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169860">Trench1419!</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-26">07/26/24 09:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ombre Nomade was the second full bottle of fragrance that I bought from the Louis Vuitton store so far.  I have six full bottles now, and 14 samples.  I love how relaxed they are at the LV store, and how they let you try out the fragrances at your leisure.  They don't care if you spray it on yourself or use the cards they also provide, and they will give you free samples if you ask.  I wish that I would have discovered the LV store sooner, because I was nervous to even look around in there at first.<br />
<br />
I'm no fragrance expert, but I can pick out the individual scent notes in some of them, like I can definitely smell the green apple top note in Pacific Chill, for example, or the salty ocean top note in City of Stars, or the sandalwood in LOVERS.  But I'm just not sure about the actual scent notes in Ombre Nomade!  I layered all of my LV scents yesterday morning, so LOVERS, Pacific Chill, Attrape-Reves, Ombre Nomade, City of Stars, and Nuit de Feu.  All day at work, I could smell Ombre Nomade, sitting at my desk.  I loved it!  There's just some scent note(s) in Ombre Nomade that really agree with my nose.  I'm not sure if it's the rose or oud or leather or what, but it smells amazing to me.<br />
<br />
It's not at all the proper temperature for Ombre Nomade here, but it seems to perform well at my indoor office job.  I don't have much of a personal life, but the one time that I got a compliment from a stranger, at the grocery store, regarding my scent, was when I had layered Ombre Nomade and Pacific Chill, and I think Mancera Instant Crush.  I was with my now ex fiance, and some other lady loudly announced that someone smelled GOOD, and asked if it was us, and my ex said that I was the one into fragrances, and the lady walked closer to us, and said that it was me, and asked what fragrances I had used.  It was pretty cool.  I've pretty much never gotten any attention from women before.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2230048"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2230048#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229757" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I don't get the fruity, sweet or rose notes whatsoever and if anyone does, I'd be amazed. Just oud, leather and the smokey note sticking out for me. Not all that interesting and certainly not worth buying a full bottle for what I'd class as quite a simplistic scent profile once it's on skin. So simplistic that you'll be able to pick this up from any number of fragrance houses without paying hundreds in cash. The notes listed at the top of the page are very misleading, but maybe my decant was from a bad batch if such a thing exists in the world of LV.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Hyper masculine not in a spicy fresh way, but a dark, menacing way. I'd imagine a full bearded, 6'2 massive man wearing this.<br />
Not a 'business man' vibe, but a 'mafia boss' vibe.<br />
I'd say unless you're 35+ and ultra rich, don't fucking wear this shit. You can't pull it off.<br />
As someone who likes sweet scents, this is awful, but I can definitely appreciate the appeal and the person who can wear this. <br />
Not worth the money, go get Pacific Chill. <br />
5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2217832"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2217832#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2216392" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It was just so obnoxious to me, which was weird because I usually like these sorts of in your face fragrances and I am also a big fan of oud. I sprayed it again today and did a complete 180. The oud rose combo is truly magic, it is very strong but to many people that's a good thing. Woody, and sweet. I can certainly pick that raspberry note out. I don't think I would wear this over my top favorites, but it is a great fragrance. If you want to stand out, likely not in a good way (this obviously is the complete opposite of mass appeal) go for this, but for the people who have the nose for it, you will stand out and they will love it. 7.5/10 for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2173632" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="LuaLat"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662645"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="LuaLat" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2173632ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2173632" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662645">LuaLat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-31">05/31/24 11:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is not to my taste and personally I would not purchase this fragrance and I do feel it is very overpriced for what it is. This is not very safe and has a low mass appeal so I would definitely recommend smelling this before purchasing and not blind buying. Strong medicinal, poison smelling very bitter Oud blended with Ambroxan, heavy dose of leather, metallic saffron and a touch of rose which is unique, mysterious and quite dark but too me smells unpleasant and something smells out of place just not right. Too me the oud here is a bit synthetic an inaccurate interpretation of Oud and I feel that this fragrance lacks depth and complexity and smells sort of one dimensional. I don’t think this is horrible but it just dosent blow me away and for this price dosent even compare competition however it is good quality, relatively smooth and I can see how others may like this scent if so then it is worth it as it performs extremely well but just don’t expect to get major compliments but it is a great fragrance for making a statement. This is also an example of very skillful and very clever perfumery as the combination of notes have been selected very well and in perfect amounts to compliment each other and this is designed to be a dark, mysterious, captivating fragrance that still has some freshness which gives it a little more versatility. <br />
<br />
In general I dislike the LV fragrances and LV as a perfume house as I feel that they are overpriced for what they are, lack character, smell generally decent at best/not mind blowing and it seems that they use their name to overcharge for fragrances that do not live up to expectations and are not as good as many fragrances from competition so apart from imagination and pacific chill which are truly wonderful fragrances I would not recommend LV as a fragrance house. <br />
<br />
Other alternatives I would recommend are <br />
<br />
Xerjoff Alexandria ii <br />
Initio Oud for greatness <br />
Thameen carved Oud <br />
<br />
As these fragrances perform just as well, they are higher quality, smell generally better and are better if you are looking for a proper oud fragrance that really set the bar for how oud is supposed to be. <br />
<br />
Due to being unique and edgy then if you do like fragrance then it is signature scent worthy for some people. <br />
<br />
Performance <br />
Longevity 12 hours on skin with projection for first 8 and 2 days longevity on clothes <br />
<br />
Projection 5 ft fills a room <br />
Village trail lingers strongly <br />
<br />
While this is not for me it is still a good fragrance and I am going to rate it as a fragrance for what it is as just because it’s not to my taste dosent mean it’s a bad fragrance you have to appreciate the work of the perfumer and other peoples enjoyment for a fragrance so I’d say it’s a 7.5 out of 10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1789480">BIGDWARF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-07">05/07/24 15:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Regarding batch differences;<br />
<br />
I got three different batches at home at the moment and have done a test were I spray a strip and put it under a glass in my bathroom (smell them everytime i go there, and they stand there for a week or so). The batches are from 20, 21 and 23. The juice is MUCH darker in the two older bottles and pretty bright in the new one. <br />
<br />
Upon smelling them under the glass, the newsest batch smells pretty alcoholy and messy, the other two smells really good and balanced. Its not until a couple of days the new batch settles into what the old batches gives you -BUT- the new batch are def more fruity than the older ones that are darker and more gasoline like. <br />
<br />
Will let the 23-batch sit for a while because its newly purchased from the LV store.<br />
<br />
Im not entirely sure about performance differences yet, but I think they are all pretty similiar and not as beastly as many people rave about. They are very strong in the beginning but has a tendency to die down rapidly after an hour or three.<br />
<br />
If you got questions, PM.<br />
<br />

Oof.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2135498"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2135498#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2134930" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2134930" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="OpiumScents"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108432"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2108432.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="OpiumScents" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2134930ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2134930" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108432">OpiumScents</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 09:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've finally been able to test this hyped fragrance. This review isn't going to be one that just going to give my opinion and completely disregard other people's views and why they may or may not like it.<br />
<br />
First of all in my opinion, its heavily overrated, and not quite the scent that oud maracuja is with the added passionfruit etc.<br />
<br />
Although the drydown is slightly better due to it imo, become slightly sweeter and fruitier, it stays pretty linear for me.<br />
<br />
I think that it's quite a harsh fragrance in terms of it being extremely in your face, almost like a metallic or burning tire sort of accord especially in the opening. <br />
<br />
The oud in this fragrance isn't working with me, it's quite a pungent, dirty and slightly animalic oud compared to ouds in actual fragrance masterpieces such as oud satin mood or roja amber aoud or even oud maracuja, it's just not a the most pleasant scent to my nose, this could also be because of the notes it's backed by, perhaps its the incense or leather accord <br />
<br />
Finally, I think it's the combination of saffron and woody notes that to my nose is gaining slight metallic note abit like in baccarat rouge 540 edp, however as a result of this which is the main reason I'm not liking this, the oud and saffron along with other notes is producing this very subtle smell which lest throughout the whole duration that smells abit like a sh*tty baby nappy that's turned slightly metallic<br />
<br />
In conclusion the scent is decent but not worth half the price, I recommened oud maracuja more between these two, however I think someone who's into really dry fragrances and is a fan of ouds that are more dirty, pungent and animalic then this is for you, or if you want to smell like your average middle eastern guy, and it is fairly mass appealing after some compliments from this scent and scent dna<br />
<br />
Scent: 6-6.5/10<br />
Projection &amp; Sillage: 9.5/10<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Price: 2/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2134930"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2134930#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2132520" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2124871" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tastysurprise"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1978586"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1978586.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tastysurprise" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Royal-Oud-12317.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12317.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Royal Oud"title="Royal Oud"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2124871ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2124871" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1978586">tastysurprise</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-14">04/14/24 17:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you love this fragrance enough to get the 200ml, then this is not overpriced per ml. It's on par with many and better than most. If you get the 100ml, then it may be overpriced but not by some ridiculous amount. So you can find fragrances that are 10% less expensive at this quality point... let's all jump up and down and scream about it! You can also find fragrances that cost 2-3x this price that are worse. It's all about what you like. <br />
<br />
This does have pretty extreme performance, and is very thick and dark. It's not for every occasion. I have a dozen fragrances at or around this price point (or much higher) and this beats most of them... whether it is the performance, or the accessibility, or the versatility, or the wearability this fragrance beats almost everything I've sampled or owned in one way or another. Two sprays maximum. You may even want to plan ahead the night before and spray the clothes you plan to wear the next day. <br />
<br />
The performance is beyond what is reasonable for most people, I'd say. You can probably find fragrances that are even more unreasonable but what would be the point of that. <br />
<br />
No way this is a unisex fragrance. Very masculine. Only by the time it has started to fade out does it come anywhere near something (I personally think could be) feminine or unisex. <br />
<br />
All that said, I love this and I think it compares favorably to strangelove deadofnight, one of my favorites, at 1/3 the cost (if you get the 200ml, which I did). But unlike that one, this is not only very wearable but has also garnered compliments on more than one occasion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2124871"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2124871#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2124050" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; That's why I rate it very high. For me however, rose is always noticeable and dominates a fragrance and I always associate it with the feminine. No matter what masculine ingredient you combine it with (oud, tobacco, patchouli, etc.) to make it more manly... I just can't picture myself wearing one of these.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2107723"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2107723#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2105077" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2105077" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DawnBreaker"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1267449"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1267449.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DawnBreaker" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Amouage/Jubilation-40-Man-87958.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.87958.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Jubilation 40 Man"title="Jubilation 40 Man"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2105077ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2105077" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1267449">DawnBreaker</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-26">03/26/24 14:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ombre Nomade seems, to me, to be aping popular pieces of other famous fragrances. Montale style oud and rose, Tuscan Leather Raspberry, Aventus birch, Amouage incense/saffron etc.. But this puts them in a single package. (Basic equasion from my perspective: Montale Aoud Night + TF Tuscan Leather = Ombre Nomade. It's kinda uncanny.) As others have said, this stuff is olfactory napalm. A single full spray is too much. And for heaven's sake, resist the urge to sniff up close. It will conquer every other scent in its vicinity. It will cling to your nose until it outstays its welcome, and still not leave. There is no escape. But seriously, I've found you almost have to apply it like an attar - a swipe behind the ears here, a dab on the hand or wrist there. If you do that you will have a very pleasant scent bubble around you. If you put on a full spray or more you will become offensive to 98% of people, yourself included. All that said, this does smell really good. It's a low key like for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2105077"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2105077#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104752" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2104752" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="POTFORTY2"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1657706"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="POTFORTY2" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2104752ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2104752" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1657706">POTFORTY2</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-26">03/26/24 09:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It’s a lot. I enjoy it quite a bit but putting in perspective that I’m blasting people with this scent is embarrassing. It’s so unique and strong most people who are not frag heads will be wondering why you’re wearing this weird smell. It’s not necessarily ‘good’ to non frag enthusiast it’s very thick raspberry rose Oud most people will not appreciate the artistry of it most will compliment you to point out they smell something that’s meant to be appealing then in secret laugh at you for wearing it in public without even knowing what you spent to smell that way. It screams ‘I’m desperate to be noticed.’<br />
<br />
I appreciate it as a frag enthusiast and I’ve been pretty bold with other scents but this one crosses the line for me. It’s the only one that’s too much. If I didn’t put into perspective the experience I’m creating for others I’d prolly love this scent and walk around with it oblivious.<br />
<br />
It MAY work on cold nights outdoors that’s such a limited scenario though it’s not versatile.<br />
<br />
If it was weaker I’d perhaps like it more but I got burned out of raspberry with Tuscan leather.<br />
<br />
Funny enough nouveau Monde is one of my all time favorites I wouldn’t wear it to work but I do wear it going out. Smells less alien more fresh easier to wear comes across like a nice leather smell. Ombré Nomade is a thick raspberry animalic rose mess IMO.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2104752"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2104752#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104439" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1416320">Itcannotalwaysbenight</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-20">03/20/24 18:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The opening is very earthy and masculine - almost too masculine and makes me wonder how this is even marketed as unisex fragrance… HOWEVER the later dry down leans feminine as the sweet florals (rose and Geranium) and fruit (raspberry) notes settle in. This totally transforms into a different fragrance about 2-3 hours after the initial spray- this one definitely requires some patience, it’s NOT a “spray and go” linear perfume. Ombre Nomade is also the complete reverse of LV Les Sables Roses which opens feminine and rosy, but dries down masculine.<br />
<br />
There’s also a subtle clean soapy note hiding in the dry down as well that makes this work in both cold and warm weather - could be the fruity raspberry and woody birch playing together? It’s very reminiscent of the fruity clean notes of Xerjoff More than Words. Either way the best way I can describe this is by spraying an ultra sweet floral perfume on an old leather jacket - just stunning and balanced! Ladies please don’t run from this because of the masculine opening- be patient and this gives super bossed up, sh*t together feminine energy. If you’re a fan of Xerjoff More Than Words or Oud Satin Mood I would categorize this a safe blind buy for those patient enough for the dry down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; If you love the overly done and boring rose / oud combo, this is the epitome. I ended up selling my Tiziana Terenzi Nero Oudh as this smells 95% the same, only difference is the dry down and quality of this is much much better. Designer better than niche??, yes. Here at least. I love when the leather comes out to play and the rose takes a back seat. The oud tries to show a bit of animatic tendencies , but never really does it. Stays oud the whole time though. This is softer and better blended and shows certain nuances from time to time. It does last a very long time and people will smell you, but I think people are being way over dramatic with it. 2-3 sprays you will be good, you’re not going to knock people down etc. it performs like a $410 fragrance with real oud should. Well done LV!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2094927"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2094927#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2094895" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is one! It’s been compared to Tom Ford’s many Oud inspired perfumes and also Dior Oud Ispahan, believe me this is head &amp; shoulders above every single one of them. I have tried oud’s from the Middle East and there are some good ones but this is better! It’s the balance, the smoothness and the sheer quality of ingredients that shine through. I don’t wear this every day and it’s better in either very hot or very cold weather, not a springtime perfume but the raspberry, benzoin, oud combination is beautiful. It lasts over a day, the sillage is enormous and the drydown is exquisite and for me the drydown has to perform and be more beautiful than the first impression.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Imagine if Tom Ford didn't make Noir de Noir. You know, with his usual unsubtle, sledgehammer on the senses approach. That's this. It's a smoother, quieter, more palatable Noir de Noir. That said, it is the same DNA for sure. If you really wanted to like Noir de Noir but found it too brash, then this might be for you. Speaking of Tom Ford, once it dries down I get a bit of the cookie accord (kulfi?) found in Noir Extreme. All in all, I think much better than Noir de Noir but it still packs a very rich punch. This is not a safe blind buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2042622"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2042622#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2041061" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1405188">rickkkkky</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-06">01/06/24 01:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The ratio of comments claiming "there's an abundance of better Middle Eastern ouds for fraction of a price" and comments actually managing to recommend even a single "better oud for fraction of a price" is very telling.<br />
<br />
Can you find Middle Eastern ouds for a fraction of the price? Absolutely. Do they serve the same function as ON? Many of them probably do. Are they better than ON in terms of the scent alone? Well, it's a subjective question, but what it's worth, I've sampled a good 60 to 80 Middle Eastern ouds (and other Western ones, too) and in my books, very few comes even close to ON - even from the pricier ones.<br />
<br />
So while you may be happy with some cheaper Middle Eastern oud (which is of course nice), the claim that there would be a plethora of better ones for a dirt cheap price is totally unwarranted.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; However I am middle eastern from the Gulf so this scent profile is quite abundant in local brands with a fraction of the price and great quality.<br />
<br />
So is it justifiable for someone like me to go and throw lots of $$$$$$$$ in something too common in our market that I can get for $ with even better quality? I think the answer is clear. <br />
<br />
I got a sample to test out and I'll keep it at that. If I used it again, then I'll layer it with some powdery perfumes to tone it down a bit as it is a bit too loud for me and it is for nighttime use. <br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868342">Garion</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-21">12/21/23 09:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have a very hard time putting my finger on what this scent is like. Someone below, one of the only few negative reviews in fact said that it smells like barnyard / fertilizer. Kinda. I get that strong damp musky smell you'd get from one of those pet shops where they sell a lot of different exotic animals like lizards, geckos, snakes, spiders etc. I'm surprised musk isn't listed as one of the main notes or accords above. It's got the longevity I wish all my favourite fragrances had. I sprayed this on my wrist last week and just put the shirt on that I was wearing that day and the sleeve is still absolutely reeking.<br />
<br />
I could enjoy this fragrance on very rare occasions where I want to smell expensive and I want everyone around me to know I smell expensive. Like for a big fund raiser. Spray it on my neck and jacket and not worry about it dying down for the next 48h. However there is something to be said for a fragrance going away eventually. Especially when it's not fresh and uplifting. If I could get a fresh spicy citrus fragrance to last like ON I'd be on it like a car bonnet.<br />
<br />
It's a tad expensive. But for the performance you will take ages getting through a bottle. Also Louis Vuitton do a refill scheme where if you bring in the bottle there's a heavy discount on refills. If you decided this was your signature scent or you were going to keep a bottle of it forever you'd get good value out of it long term. Cost is high to try, cheap to keep.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="2007042"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=2007042#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2006930" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1356676">cat1994</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-06-29">06/29/21 16:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My absolute favourite of all time and my signature scent -- love at first sniff. <br />
<br />
On my skin, it develops like creamy, woody goodness. Rich. Pure luxury. Beautiful scent from first spray. Never fails to get compliments (and being stopped on the street and asked what I'm wearing!). <br />
<br />
It's versatile -- I wear it both during day and night, but do tend to keep it to night in summer months. It lasts ages both on the skin and on clothes and bedding. Sometimes stays in clothes even after being washed (some may not find this appealing but I personally do, as it provides the right amount of scent if I don't want to add any more). <br />
<br />
The last time I went home, over a year and a half ago, I borrowed my mum's jacket and -- believe it or not -- all this time later she says she hasn't taken it to the cleaners as it still smells like me (though quite faintly, of course). <br />
<br />
I truly have no words for how utterly excellent this perfume is. A genius creation I cannot recommend enough. If you can only have one perfume from LV, let it be this one. Ask for a sample and let your senses run wild. A perfect 10/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49755"comment_id="1368016"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Ombre-Nomade-49755.html?ccid=1368016#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1116136" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1581757" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1581757" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="VETTIVAER"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1436289"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="VETTIVAER" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1581757ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1581757" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1436289">VETTIVAER</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-06-10">06/10/22 10:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I tried this fragrance from an official boutique, both on skin and paper. I give you only my honest review below.<br />
<br />
Ombre Nomade is often discussed in the fragrance community as THE reference modern rose oud scent. After trying Armani Prive, BDK, and a number of other designer, niche and indie ouds/rose-ouds,  I was beyond excited to finally try ON. I walked into the Louis V boutique in Florence, Italy, ready to drop the euros if the scent is agreeable in person. <br />
<br />
Initially, the olfactory impression was identical to the leather component of Tuscan Leather by Tom Ford (minus the raspberries), with the projection dial turned up to 11/10. <br />
<br />
I had not expected this to be a leather forward scent (on the test strip and on skin!). To double check, I asked my partner, who were not aware of this fragrance. They confirmed my impression. <br />
<br />
The hyper-diffusive Tuscan leather effect continued for roughly 6 hours in hot Italian weather, while slowly fading throughout. Here comes the most disappointing part:<br />
<br />
Simultaneously as the leather note fades, a dry, cheap, generic synthetic backbone becomes apparent. To me it smells identical to the aromachemical norlimbanol (dry, peppery, diffusive synthetic driftwood note, popularly abused in modern mens' fragrances to add projection). I did not expect such a cheap synthetic buzz from what is a $400 fragrance. <br />
<br />
First the disappointment with it being a leather fragrance, and now the cheap smelling base. I was glad I saved myself hundreds of Euros. I ended up picking up an indie spicy leather scent that I had sampled instead, which costs half as much, smells much smoother, more complex, and performs all day.<br />
<br />
How did this cheap smelling scent get such rave reviews in the community? Probably the same way brown checkered leather purses with 'LV' stamped on them sell for tens of thousands of Euros. 100% hype and status symbol. <br />
<br />
Better options for the price: Armani Prive Oud Royale, Armani Prive Rose d'Arabie, BDK Abramad, Aqua Flor Aoud, offerings from Arabian Oud.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
